class="component title">\r\n  <h2 id="key-economic-reports-and-factors-that-move-markets" class="title-text none crmt-2">\r\n    \r\n      Key economic reports and factors that move markets\r\n      \r\n    \r\n  </h2>\r\n</div>\r\n\r\n\r\n<div class="row  big-gutters justify-content-start crmt-3 ">\r\n  <div class="col-md-6">\r\n\r\n  \r\n  <div class="cq-placeholder cq-marker-start" data-emptytext="Expand/Collapse"></div>\r\n<div class="component react expand-collapse None" data-is-edit="false" data-collapse-at="alwaysEnable" data-component-title="Non-Farm Payroll" data-list-style="default" data-title-type="h5">\r\n  <div path="expand-collapse-elements">\r\n\r\n  \r\n  <div class="cmp cmp-text">\r\n<div class="component react text">\r\n  <div path="text">\r\n    \r\n      <p>This monthly report shows changes in U.S. jobs, drives Fed policy and indicates economic growth.</p>\n\r\n    \r\n  </div>\r\n</div>\r\n\n    \n\r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n</div>\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n</div>\r\n</div>\r\n\r\n  \r\n<link as="style" href="/etc.clientlibs/cmegroupaem/clientlibs/expand-collapse.861f54574349b356209161c6a08881a4.css" media="all" onload="this.onload=null;this.rel=\'stylesheet\'" rel="preload" type="text/css">\n\n<script async="true" src="/etc.clientlibs/cmegroupaem/clientlibs/expand-collapse.476eaaaa7741ace6b63dec586c5a6809.js"></script>\n\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n<div class="component divider line always">\r\n  <hr class="left full-width gray3 "/>\r\n</div><div class="cq-placeholder cq-marker-start" data-emptytext="Expand/Collapse"></div>\r\n<div class="component react expand-collapse None" data-is-edit="false" data-collapse-at="alwaysEnable" data-component-title="Unemployment reports" data-list-style="default" data-title-type="h5">\r\n  <div path="expand-collapse-elements">\r\n\r\n  \r\n  <div class="cmp cmp-text">\r\n<div class="component react text">\r\n  <div path="text">\r\n    \r\n      <p>These reports present the U.S. unemployment rate as a percentage. They drive Fed policy and indicate economys strength.</p>\n\r\n    \r\n  </div>\r\n</div>\r\n\n    \n\r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n</div>\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n</div>\r\n</div>\r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n<div class="component divider line always">\r\n  <hr class="left full-width gray3 "/>\r\n</div><div class="cq-placeholder cq-marker-start" data-emptytext="Expand/Collapse"></div>\r\n<div class="component react expand-collapse None" data-is-edit="false" data-collapse-at="alwaysEnable" data-component-title="Earnings releases" data-list-style="default" data-title-type="h5">\r\n  <div path="expand-collapse-elements">\r\n\r\n  \r\n  <div class="cmp cmp-text">\r\n<div class="component react text">\r\n  <div path="text">\r\n    \r\n      <p>These updates list changes in earnings of publically traded companies, which can move the market.</p>\n\r\n    \r\n  </div>\r\n</div>\r\n\n    \n\r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n</div>\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n</div>\r\n</div>\r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n<div class="component divider line always">\r\n  <hr class="left full-width gray3 "/>\r\n</div><div class="cq-placeholder cq-marker-start" data-emptytext="Expand/Collapse"></div>\r\n<div class="component react expand-collapse None" data-is-edit="false" data-collapse-at="alwaysEnable" data-component-title="FOMC (Federal Open Markets Committee)" data-list-style="default" data-title-type="h5">\r\n  <div path="expand-collapse-elements">\r\n\r\n  \r\n  <div class="cmp cmp-text">\r\n<div class="component react text">\r\n  <div path="text">\r\n    \r\n      <p>The Federal Open Market Committee determines U.S. monetary policy and whether to move the key interest rate. It also drives stock market movements.</p>\n\r\n    \r\n  </div>\r\n</div>\r\n\n    \n\r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n</div>\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n</div>\r\n</div>\r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n<div class="component divider line always">\r\n  <hr class="left full-width gray3 "/>\r\n</div>\r\n  \r\n\r\n</div>\n<div class="col-md-6">\r\n\r\n  \r\n  <div class="cq-placeholder cq-marker-start" data-emptytext="Expand/Collapse"></div>\r\n<div class="component react expand-collapse None" data-is-edit="false" data-collapse-at="alwaysEnable" data-component-title="CPI (Consumer Price Index)" data-list-style="default" data-title-type="h5">\r\n  <div path="expand-collapse-elements">\r\n\r\n  \r\n  <div class="cmp cmp-text">\r\n<div class="component react text">\r\n  <div path="text">\r\n    \r\n      <p>The Consumer Price Index measures inflation or cost-of-living changes through average price of a basket of goods and services.</p>\n\r\n    \r\n  </div>\r\n</div>\r\n\n    \n\r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n</div>\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n</div>\r\n</div>\r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n<div class="component divider line always">\r\n  <hr class="left full-width gray3 "/>\r\n</div><div <div class="col">\r\n\r\n  \r\n  \r\n<div class="component title">\r\n  <h2 id="about-e-mini-sp-500" class="title-text none crmt-2">\r\n    \r\n      About E-mini S&amp;P 500\r\n      \r\n    \r\n  </h2>\r\n</div>\r\n<div class="cmp cmp-text">\r\n<div class="component react text">\r\n  <div path="text">\r\n    \r\n      <p>An electronically traded futures contract one fifth the size of standard S&amp;P futures, E-mini S&amp;P 500 futures and options are based on the underlying Standard &amp; Poors 500 stock index. Made up of 500 individual stocks representing the market capitalizations of large companies, the S&amp;P 500 Index is a leading indicator of large-cap U.S. equities.\xa0</p>\n\r\n    \r\n path="afterContent">\n\n\n\n\n    \n    \n    \r\n\r\n<div class="row  justify-content-start crmb-4 ">\r\n  <div class="col">\r\n\r\n  \r\n  \r\n<div class="component title">\r\n  <h2 id="about-e-mini-sp-500" class="title-text none crmt-2">\r\n    \r\n      About E-mini S&amp;P 500\r\n      \r\n    \r\n  </h2>\r\n</div>\r\n<div class="cmp cmp-text">\r\n<div class="component react text">\r\n  <div path="text">\r\n    \r\n      <p>An electronically traded futures contract one fifth the size of standard S&amp;P futures, E-mini S&amp;P 500 futures and options are based on the underlying Standard &amp; Poors 500 stock index. Made up of 500 individual stocks representing the market capitalizations of large companies, the S&amp;P 500 Index is a leading indicator of large-cap U.S. equities.\xa0</p>\n\r\n    \r\n
